Pwnab1e


#include <bits/stdc++.h>
#define kN 1000001
#define oo 1000000007
#define int long long
#define double long double
#define fast ios::sync_with_stdio(0), cin.tie(0)
#define endl '\n'
using namespace std;

int gcd(int a, int b){
    if(a<=0||b<=0)exit(1);
    int c=a%b;
    return c?gcd(b, c):b;
}

int lcm(int a, int b){
    return a*b/gcd(a, b);
}

int a[1000000], n;
struct seg{
    int l, r, m, v;
    seg *cl=NULL, *cr=NULL;
    seg(){}
    seg(int _l, int _r){
        l=_l, r=_r, m=l+r>>1;
        if(r-l>1)cl=new seg(l, m), cr=new seg(m, r), pull();
        else v=a[l];
    }
    void pull(){
        v=lcm(cl->v, cr->v);
    }
    void add(int id){
        if(r-l==1){++v; return;}
        if(id<m)cl->add(id);
        else cr->add(id);
        pull();
    }
    int qry(int _l, int _r){
        if(_l<=l&&r<=_r)return v;
        int ret=1;
        if(_l<m)ret=lcm(ret, cl->qry(_l, _r));
        if(m<_r)ret=lcm(ret, cr->qry(_l, _r));
        return ret;
    }
};

signed main(){
    //fast;
    for(int i=0; i<kN; ++i)a[i]=1;
    cin>>n;
    if(n>kN)exit(1);
    seg *root=new seg(0, n);
    int q;
    cin>>q;
    if(q>10)exit(1);
    while(q--){
        int id;
        cin>>id;
        if(id<0||id>=n)exit(1);
        root->add(id);
    }
    int l, r;
    cin>>l>>r;
    if(l<0||r>n||l>=r)exit(1);
    if(root->qry(l, r)>6666666)out_flag();
    else out_fake_flag();
    system("PAUSE");
    return 0;
}
